## 2. L0_CONSTITUTIONAL (Core, Types, Safety) (100 Directives)

- **Criticality:** DAL-A / CRITICAL
- **STAMP Mapping:** `SC-INFO-099` (Unsafe Control Action / Process Model Flaw)
- **Information Metrics:** H(source)=6.918, I(source;target)=1.123, Loss=5.795 bits
- **FMEA Analysis:**
  - *Failure Mode:* Agent misapplies Cryptographic Nonces during `System.Uri` translation, causing structural divergence in `Dict`.
  - *Effect:* Data corruption enters the system at the lowest boundary via `Dict`. Shannon entropy of state space exceeds safe bounds (H=6.92 bits).
  - *Mitigation (MSTS):* Implement MSTS `<morphism>` tag. Validate `Dict` structural integrity. Prove Hoare preconditions. Verify H(X|Y) <= 0.86 bits for SIL-6 compliance.
